Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





PDFium uses Little-CMS to support ICC profiles. I used AFLSmart fuzzer to fuzz the library and I found a SEGV that causes the test program to crash. I have attached a fuzzed ICC profile that can trigger the bug and following is what ASAN says. It seems to me that there is something wrong in the cmsReadTag function.



<span class="line"><!---->PDFium uses Little-CMS to support ICC profiles. I used AFLSmart fuzzer to fuzz the library and I found a SEGV that causes the test program to crash. I have attached a fuzzed ICC profile that can trigger the bug and following is what ASAN says. It seems to me that there is something wrong in the cmsReadTag function.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Normally ASAN says something like this -- indicating that is is a NULL pointer dereference



<span class="line"><!---->Normally ASAN says something like this -- indicating that is is a NULL pointer dereference<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>

REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





Use the following test driver



<span class="line"><!---->Use the following test driver<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





#include <stdint.h>



<span class="line"><!---->#include &lt;stdint.h&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





#include "lcms2.h"



<span class="line"><!---->#include "lcms2.h"<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





void ReadAllTags(cmsHPROFILE h) {



<span class="line"><!---->void ReadAllTags(cmsHPROFILE h) {<!----></span>



<br>





    cmsInt32Number i, n;



<span class="line"><!---->    cmsInt32Number i, n;<!----></span>



<br>





    cmsTagSignature sig;



<span class="line"><!---->    cmsTagSignature sig;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





    n = cmsGetTagCount(h);



<span class="line"><!---->    n = cmsGetTagCount(h);<!----></span>



<br>





    for (i=0; i < n; i++) {



<span class="line"><!---->    for (i=0; i &lt; n; i++) {<!----></span>



<br>





        sig = cmsGetTagSignature(h, i);



<span class="line"><!---->        sig = cmsGetTagSignature(h, i);<!----></span>



<br>





        if (cmsReadTag(h, sig) == NULL) return;



<span class="line"><!---->        if (cmsReadTag(h, sig) == NULL) return;<!----></span>



<br>





    }



<span class="line"><!---->    }<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





int main(int argc, char* argv[]) {



<span class="line"><!---->int main(int argc, char* argv[]) {<!----></span>



<br>





  cmsHPROFILE h = cmsOpenProfileFromFile(argv[1], "rb");



<span class="line"><!---->  cmsHPROFILE h = cmsOpenProfileFromFile(argv[1], "rb");<!----></span>



<br>





  if (!h) return 0;



<span class="line"><!---->  if (!h) return 0;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  ReadAllTags(h);



<span class="line"><!---->  ReadAllTags(h);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  cmsCloseProfile(h);



<span class="line"><!---->  cmsCloseProfile(h);<!----></span>



<br>





  return 0;



<span class="line"><!---->  return 0;<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>

UndefinedBehaviorSanitizer:DEADLYSIGNAL



<span class="line"><!---->UndefinedBehaviorSanitizer:DEADLYSIGNAL<!----></span>



<br>





ERROR: UndefinedBehaviorSanitizer: SEGV on unknown address 0x7fbd094f41ba (pc 0x7fbc0a12c1e3 bp 0x7ffc20fa1da0 sp 0x7ffc20fa1d58 T436118)



<span class="line"><!---->ERROR: UndefinedBehaviorSanitizer: SEGV on unknown address 0x7fbd094f41ba (pc 0x7fbc0a12c1e3 bp 0x7ffc20fa1da0 sp 0x7ffc20fa1d58 T436118)<!----></span>



<br>





The signal is caused by a READ memory access.



<span class="line"><!---->The signal is caused by a READ memory access.<!----></span>



<br>





    #0 0x7fbc0a12c1e3  string/../sysdeps/x86_64/multiarch/memmove-vec-unaligned-erms.S:391



<span class="line"><!---->    #0 0x7fbc0a12c1e3  string/../sysdeps/x86_64/multiarch/memmove-vec-unaligned-erms.S:391<!----></span>



<br>





    #1 0x557db3b2881e in MemoryRead cmsio0.c



<span class="line"><!---->    #1 0x557db3b2881e in MemoryRead cmsio0.c<!----></span>

I actually think this is Security_Severity=None. If this issue really affected PDFium, PDFium's pdf_codec_icc_fuzzer would have likely found it a long time ago. The reason it cannot happen is Little CMS never calls cmsReadTag() with cmsSigUcrBgTag. All the calls to cmsReadTag() are either:



<span class="line"><!---->I actually think this is Security_Severity=None. If this issue really affected PDFium, PDFium's pdf_codec_icc_fuzzer would have likely found it a long time ago. The reason it cannot happen is Little CMS never calls cmsReadTag() with cmsSigUcrBgTag. All the calls to cmsReadTag() are either:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1) For specific signature, none of which is cmsSigUcrBgTag.



<span class="line"><!---->1) For specific signature, none of which is cmsSigUcrBgTag.<!----></span>



<br>





2) For a variable, but the variable always comes from a constant lookup table like `Device2PCS16` from cmsio1.c. These never contain cmsSigUcrBgTag.



<span class="line"><!---->2) For a variable, but the variable always comes from a constant lookup table like `Device2PCS16` from cmsio1.c. These never contain cmsSigUcrBgTag.<!----></span>



<br>





3) From cmsReadRawTag(), which takes an arbitrary signature. PDFium never calls cmsReadRawTag().



<span class="line"><!---->3) From cmsReadRawTag(), which takes an arbitrary signature. PDFium never calls cmsReadRawTag().<!----></span>

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }

          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
      </style>
      <div class="chops-autocomplete-container">
        <span class="screenreader-hidden" aria-live="polite">
          
        </span>
        <table hidden="">
          <tbody>
            
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    <!----></mr-autocomplete>
            </div>
          </div>

      <style>

 let cl = new ClientLogger("issues");
 if (cl.started("new-issue")) {
 cl.logEnd("new-issue", null, 120 * 1000);
 }
 if (cl.started("issue-search")) {
 cl.logEnd("issue-search");
 }
 }
 });
